background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">i have a folder called lib at the repo root. there are js files inside, like foo bar whatever. how to use wildcard to match them all and use pnpm link to install them, without manually naming each explicitly or writing automation scripts. then i could import "lib/foo" anywhere in the repo.</span><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: center; height: fit-content; margin-left: 8px; margin-top: auto; display: flex; flex: 1 1 auto; place-content: end; outline: 0px;"><div style="color: rgb(139, 140, 145); height: 14px; margin-bottom: 2px; rotate: 180deg; display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">To link multiple local files or packages using&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;without manually naming each one, you should use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">pnpm workspaces</span>&nbsp;with a wildcard configuration. This is the standard way to handle "bulk" internal linking without custom scripts.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Configure the Workspace<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Create a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code>&nbsp;file at your repo root. This tells&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;to treat every folder or valid package inside&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/</code>&nbsp;as a local dependency.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">yaml</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;"># pnpm-workspace.yaml</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">packages</span><span>:
  - </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'.'</span><span>      </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;"># The root project</span><span>
  - </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'lib/*'</span><span>  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;"># All folders inside lib</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Prepare the Files<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">For&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;to recognize them, each item in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/</code>&nbsp;must be a directory containing a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>. If you currently only have flat&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.js</code>&nbsp;files, you must wrap them:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Move&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.js</code>&nbsp;to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo/index.js</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Add a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo/package.json</code>&nbsp;with&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">{"name": "lib/foo", "version": "0.0.0"}</code>.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Link them All<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Once the workspace is defined, you can "link" all of them to your root (or any other package in the repo) using a wildcard in your shell. Run this from your project root:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">bash</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code>pnpm add lib/*
</code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">What this does:</span>&nbsp;It tells&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;to find every package inside the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/</code>&nbsp;directory and add it to your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;as a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">workspace:</code>&nbsp;dependency.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Result:</span>&nbsp;Your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;will now contain:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"dependencies"</span><span>: {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/foo"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"workspace:*"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/bar"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"workspace:*"</span><span>
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 62.7344px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. Import Anywhere<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">After running&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm install</code>, you can import these anywhere in your repo just as you requested:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.2031px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">YouTube</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> foo </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'lib/foo'</span><span>;
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Alternative (No Wildcard Support):</span>&nbsp;If your shell doesn't support the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">*</code>&nbsp;wildcard for the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">add</code>&nbsp;command, you can use the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://pnpm.io/cli/link" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; method is the recommended way to manage internal "lib" folders at scale.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Folder Structure</span>: Each "package" must be in its own folder (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo/</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/bar/</code>). If your files are flat (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.js</code>), you must move them into folders with an&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">index.js</code>&nbsp;or specify a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">main</code>&nbsp;field.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">package.json</span>: Each subfolder inside&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/</code>&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">must</span>&nbsp;have its own&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;file with a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">name</code>&nbsp;(e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">"name": "lib/foo"</code>) for&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;to recognize it as a package.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Importing<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Once added,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm</code>&nbsp;creates the symlinks in your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>. You can then import them using the name defined in the subfolder's&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> foo </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'lib/foo'</span><span>;
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Note:</span>&nbsp;If you are using&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">TypeScript</span>, you will also need to add a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">paths</code>&nbsp;mapping in your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code>&nbsp;so the editor recognizes these local links:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex;   </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"paths"</span><span>: {

  }

background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder as a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">single local package</span>&nbsp;and use the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;field with a wildcard pattern.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; Create a Package in the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;Folder<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;inside your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/</code>&nbsp;directory to define it as a linkable package.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">File:</span>&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/package.json</code><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"name"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"version"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"0.0.0"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"type"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"module"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"exports"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*.js"</span><span>
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Wildcard</span>:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">"./*": "./*.js"</code>&nbsp;maps any subpath import like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo</code>&nbsp;directly to the file&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.js</code>.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 75.9375px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">webpack</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Link the Library to Your Project<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">From your&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">repository root</span>, run the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link</code>&nbsp;command to point your project's&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>&nbsp;to that local folder.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">bash</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code>pnpm link ./lib
</code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Usage<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Now you can import any file within that folder from anywhere in your repo:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// This resolves to your-repo/lib/foo.js</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> foo </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/foo"</span><span>; 

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// This resolves to your-repo/lib/bar.js</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> bar </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/bar"</span><span>;
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why this works<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Encapsulation</span>: The&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;field defines exactly which files are accessible. By using&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">./*</code>, you allow any file in that directory to be reached via a subpath.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Symlinking</span>:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link</code>&nbsp;creates a symlink in your root&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules/lib</code>&nbsp;that points to your local&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">./lib</code>&nbsp;folder.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">No Workspaces</span>: This method treats&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;as a standard local dependency without needing a complex&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code>&nbsp;setup.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 63.2734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">A Note for TypeScript Users<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If you use TypeScript, you must also tell the compiler where to find these files, as it doesn't always resolve&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;in local links automatically:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">File:</span>&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"compilerOptions"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"paths"</span><span>: {
      </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/*"</span><span>: [</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./lib/*"</span><span>]
    }
  }
}

The&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">wildcard export + link</span>&nbsp;method reduces your maintenance to just&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">one file</span>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">one command</span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">To make this work with TypeScript, you need to ensure two things: that the TS compiler understands the&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;field in your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;and that your IDE (like VS Code) can find the source files for "go-to-definition" support.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Update your Root&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">TypeScript requires a modern&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">moduleResolution</code>&nbsp;setting to recognize the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;field from a linked package.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"compilerOptions"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">/* 1. Tell TS how to resolve the 'exports' field */</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"moduleResolution"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"NodeNext"</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// or "Bundler" if you use Vite/Webpack/Esbuild</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"module"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"NodeNext"</span><span>,

    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">/* 2. Map the imports to your local source for editor support */</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"baseUrl"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"."</span><span>,
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"paths"</span><span>: {
      </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/*"</span><span>: [</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./lib/*"</span><span>]
    },

    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">/* 3. Ensure TS can see the JS files if they aren't .ts yet */</span><span>
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"allowJs"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">true</span><span>,
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"checkJs"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">false</span><span>
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Add Type Definitions (Optional but Recommended)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If your files are&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.js</code>, you can still get full type safety by creating a matching&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.d.ts</code>&nbsp;file for each JS file. For example, if you have&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.js</code>, you can add&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.d.ts</code>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If you want to handle types for the entire folder at once, update your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/package.json</code>:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"name"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"version"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"0.0.0"</span><span>,

</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Verification Steps<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Restart TS Server</span>: In VS Code, open the Command Palette (<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">Ctrl+Shift+P</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">Cmd+Shift+P</code>) and run&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">"TypeScript: Restart TS Server"</span>. This forces it to re-read the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">paths</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Test Import</span>: Type&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">import foo from "lib/foo";</code>&nbsp;in a project file.</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If it has a red squiggle, check that&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">moduleResolution</code>&nbsp;is correctly set to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">NodeNext</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">Bundler</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">If you can't "Cmd+Click" to open the file, double-check that your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">paths</code>&nbsp;in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code>&nbsp;matches the relative path to your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul></li></ol><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Why this is best:</span>&nbsp;This combination allows&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Node.js to handle the runtime resolution</span>&nbsp;via&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>, while&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.typescriptlang.org/tsconfig/paths.html" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2);
