font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">can it load all files without prefix in lib without manually naming them</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">To import all files from&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;without a prefix (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">import { x } from 'foo'</code>) and without manually naming each file,&nbsp;<mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;">you can use a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">post-install symlink script</span></mark>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Node.js strictly requires every "bare" import (one without a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">/</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">./</code>) to correspond to a folder in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>. To automate this for every file in your folder, follow these steps:<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 69.9922px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Node.js</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. The Automation Script<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Create a file named&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">setup-lib.js</code>&nbsp;in your project root. This script will automatically look at your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder and create a "fake" package in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>&nbsp;for every file it finds.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> fs </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'node:fs'</span><span>;
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> path </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'node:path'</span><span>;

</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> libDir = path.resolve(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'lib'</span><span>);
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> nodeModulesDir = path.resolve(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'node_modules'</span><span>);

</span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Get all .js files in lib</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> files = fs.readdirSync(libDir).filter(f =&gt; f.endsWith(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'.js'</span><span>));

files.forEach(file =&gt; {
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> fileName = path.parse(file).name; </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 'foo' from 'foo.js'</span><span>
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> targetDir = path.join(nodeModulesDir, fileName);

  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 1. Create a folder in node_modules for the "package"</span><span>
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">if</span><span> (!fs.existsSync(targetDir)) fs.mkdirSync(targetDir, { recursive: </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">true</span><span> });

  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// 2. Create a package.json so Node sees it as a module</span><span>
  </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">const</span><span> pkgJson = {
    name: fileName,
    version: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"1.0.0"</span><span>,
    </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">type</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"module"</span><span>,
    main: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">`../../lib/${</span><span>file</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">}`</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Point back to your actual file</span><span>
  };

  fs.writeFileSync(
    path.join(targetDir, </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'package.json'</span><span>), 
    JSON.stringify(pkgJson, </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">null</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">2</span><span>)
  );
});

console.log(</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">`Linked ${</span><span>files.length</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">} files from lib/ as top-level modules.`</span><span>);
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Automate with pnpm<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Add this script to your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;under the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">scripts</code>&nbsp;section. Use the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">postinstall</code>&nbsp;hook so it runs every time you run&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm install</code>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 57.4219px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Medium</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;"></span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"scripts"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"postinstall"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"node setup-lib.js"</span><span>
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Usage<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Run&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm install</code>&nbsp;once to trigger the script. Now, whenever you add a file like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/helper.js</code>, simply re-run&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm install</code>&nbsp;(or the script directly) and you can import it immediately:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">javascript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { myFunc } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'foo'</span><span>;    </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// from lib/foo.js</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { util } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'helper'</span><span>;   </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// from lib/helper.js</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Why this is the only way for "No Prefix"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Node.js Resolution</span>: Node only looks for bare names in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Wildcard Limits</span>: Wildcards in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;"exports"&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">always</span>&nbsp;require the package name as a prefix (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo</code>).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Dynamic Links</span>: This script effectively "fakes" a separate pnpm installation for every single file in your folder automatically.</span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 91.3125px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stanley Ulili</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Note:</span>&nbsp;Since these links are generated in your local&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">node_modules</code>, ensure you do&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">not</span>&nbsp;ignore&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">setup-lib.js</code>&nbsp;so other developers can generate the same environment.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you Configure the Workspace<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Update your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code>&nbsp;file at the root of your monorepo to include all subdirectories of&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;as part of the workspace.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">yaml</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(250, 144, 62);">packages</span><span>:
  - </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'apps/*'</span><span>
  - </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'packages/*'</span><span>
  - </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'lib/*'</span><span>  </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;"># This tells pnpm that every folder in /lib is a package</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Add package.json to each Lib<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Every subfolder (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo</code>,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/bar</code>) must have its own&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>. Use a consistent naming convention like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">@my-repo/foo</code>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 63.0703px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">lib/foo/package.json</span>:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"name"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"@my-repo/foo"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"version"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"1.0.0"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"main"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./index.ts"</span><span> 
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Link and Import<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Instead of using relative paths like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">../../lib/foo</code>, you can now "install" these local libraries into any other app or package in your repo using the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">workspace:*</code>&nbsp;protocol.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 63.0703px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Add the dependency</span>:<br>Run this from the package where you want to use the lib:<br><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm add @my-repo/foo --workspace</code></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Import normally</span>:<br>Now you can import from anywhere in the monorepo using the clean alias:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">typescript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { something } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'@my-repo/foo'</span><span>;
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">4. Enable TypeScript Support (Optional)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">To ensure your IDE (like VS Code) recognizes these imports without needing a build step, define&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">path aliases</span>&nbsp;in your root&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"compilerOptions"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"baseUrl"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"."</span><span>,
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"paths"</span><span>: {
      </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"@my-repo/*"</span><span>: [</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/*"</span><span>]
    }
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like help setting up a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">shared TypeScript configuration</span>&nbsp;that all these libraries can inherit from?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div><svg fill="currentColor" width="20px" height="20px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 -1 13 18"><path d="M1.77734 2.96289C2.10462 2.96289 2.37012 3.22838 2.37012 3.55566C2.37003 3.86235 2.13657 4.11509 1.83789 4.14551L1.7168 4.15137C1.41824 4.18181 1.18479 4.43369 1.18457 line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; padding: 12px 16px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; max-inline-size: 472px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">use wildcard to load all files in lib. lib contains files, not folders. use link to install them.</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">In a&nbsp;</div><span style="font-weight: 700;">pnpm monorepo</span>, pnpm's workspace engine is designed to manage&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">folders</span>&nbsp;containing a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>&nbsp;as packages. It does not natively support treating individual&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">files</span>&nbsp;as separate workspace packages using wildcards in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code>.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">However, you can achieve your goal of importing&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/foo.ts</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/bar.ts</code>&nbsp;from anywhere without manual relative paths by using&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">TypeScript Path Mapping</span>&nbsp;or a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Single Entry Package</span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Option 1: TypeScript Path Mapping (Recommended)<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">This is the standard way to alias a directory of files so they are available globally in your monorepo without relative paths.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Update your root&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">tsconfig.json</code></span>:<br>Define a wildcard path that maps to your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder.</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"compilerOptions"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"baseUrl"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"."</span><span>,
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"paths"</span><span>: {
      </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"@lib/*"</span><span>: [</span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"lib/*"</span><span>]
    }
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Usage</span>:<br>Now, in any file in any app (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">apps/web/src/index.ts</code>), you can import directly:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">typescript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { something } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'@lib/foo'</span><span>; </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Resolves to lib/foo.ts</span><span>
</span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { other } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'@lib/bar'</span><span>;     </span><span style="color: rgb(154, 160, 166); font-style: italic;">// Resolves to lib/bar.ts</span><span>
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Option 2: The "Single Lib" Workspace Package<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">If you want to use the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">link</code>&nbsp;behavior specifically (pnpm's&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">workspace:*</code>&nbsp;protocol), treat the entire&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder as one package and use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">Subpath Exports</span>.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Create&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/package.json</code></span>:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"name"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"@my-repo/lib"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"version"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"1.0.0"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"exports"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*.ts"</span><span>
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Link it</span>:<br>In your other apps, add the dependency:<br><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm add @my-repo/lib --workspace</code></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Usage</span>:</span><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">typescript</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">import</span><span> { something } </span><span style="color: rgb(197, 138, 249);">from</span><span> </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">'@my-repo/lib/foo'</span><span>;
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ol><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">Summary of Wildcards in&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm-workspace.yaml</code>&nbsp;(e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">- 'lib/*'</code>) only works if each item matched is a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">directory</span>&nbsp;containing a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>. It will ignore standalone&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.ts</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">.js</code>&nbsp;files.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 96.3516px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><div style="display: contents;">To import individual files from a&nbsp;</div><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder as separate entry points, you can use the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code></span>&nbsp;wildcard in your&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/package.json</code>&nbsp;and then use&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link</code>&nbsp;to make it available to your other packages.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Configure&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib/package.json</code><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Add the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">exports</code>&nbsp;field with a wildcard pattern. This tells Node.js and pnpm that any file in the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder can be imported directly as a subpath.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.7734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div style="margin-block: 24px 32px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><div><div style="background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 16px 16px 4px 4px; overflow: auto hidden; padding: 12px 16px 0px;"><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="font-family: var(--Eou8Yc); font-size: var(--GiToJf); line-height: var(--qWZYEc); letter-spacing: 0px;">json</div></div><div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; overflow-x: auto;"><pre><code><span>{
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"name"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"@my-repo/lib"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"version"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"1.0.0"</span><span>,
  </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"exports"</span><span>: {
    </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*"</span><span>: </span><span style="color: rgb(129, 201, 149);">"./*.ts"</span><span>
  }
}
</span></code></pre></div></div><div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px 4px 16px 16px; margin-top: 3px; overflow: hidden; padding: 0px 16px; height: 48px;"><div style="font-size: 12px;">Use code with caution.</div><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M360-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T280-320v-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T360-880h360q33 0 56.5 23.5T800-800v480q0 33-23.5 56.5T720-240H360Zm0-80h360v-480H360v480ZM200-80q-33 0-56.5-23.5T120-160v-560h80v560h440v80H200Zm160-240v-480 480Z"></path></svg></div></div></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><em style="font-weight: inherit;">Note: If your files are already compiled to JS, change the extension to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">./*.js</code>.</em><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Link the Library<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">You have two ways to "install" this link so it's available everywhere.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 60.6797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Option A: Global Link (Manual)</span><br>Use this if you want the link to persist across your entire machine without modifying every&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">package.json</code>.</span><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Go to the lib folder:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">cd lib</code></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Register it globally:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link --global</code></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Go to your app:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">cd ../apps/my-app</code></span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Connect it:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link --global @my-repo/lib</code></span></li></ol></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Option B: Relative Link (Recommended for Monorepos)</span><br>This creates a local symlink directly between folders.</span><ol style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 20px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">From your app folder (e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">apps/my-app</code>):</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: decimal; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">Run:&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">pnpm link ../../lib</code></span><span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 63.2734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">PNPM</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ol></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Usage<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="text-wrap: nowrap; position: relative;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Now you can import any file from the&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">lib</code>&nbsp;folder using the clean&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">@my-repo/lib/filename</code>&nbsp;syntax without relative paths.<span><span style="text-wrap: nowrap;
